# ::id dip_test_0001.1
# ::snt Hey Austria! I know AT is one of the least successful alliances in the game, so I'm super down to work together here, especially if we can get Russia and Turkey fighting.
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (a / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a2 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Austria")))
            :ARG3 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Russia"))
                  :op2 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Turkey"))))
      :ARG3 c2)
